# CARPRO Iron X\n\nBrand: Carpro\n\nRegular price: $24.95 CAD\nSale price: $21.21 CAD (Save $3.74)\n\nSizes:\n- 500ml - $21.21 CAD\n- 1L - $39.95 CAD\n- 4L - $139.95 CAD\n\n3%+ Discount with 3+ of the Same Item\n\nBarcode (500ml): 8809397811051\nBarcode (1L): 8809397811068\nBarcode (4L): 8809397811075\n\n## Easily removes iron particles\nIronX works by creating a water-soluble complex with iron particles lodged in the surface, facilitating their removal through rinsing. This process provides a deeper cleaning compared to washing or claying alone.\nThe new formula features a reduced odor compared to others on the market.\n\nSafe and pH Neutral\nIronX features an advanced pH-balanced (pH-7) formula that safely breaks down ferrous metallic contamination caused by automotive brakes, rail travel, and construction from delicate vehicle surfaces. It can be used on paint, plastic, chrome, glass, and alloy wheels.\n\nStrong and fast decon\nUse CARPRO IronX as part of the chemical decontamination process, right before the initial wash. Always work on a cool panel and avoid direct sunlight. On hot days, work in sections and do not allow the product to dry.\n\nIt's important to note that IronX does not replace clay bars but complements them. IronX helps remove the majority of contaminants, making the clay bar process safer.\n\n# CarPro IronX Cherry (Low Odor Ver.)\n\n### Highly effective, acid-free and pH balanced (6~7pH) car paint, wheels & glass cleaner\n\nSafe for all wheels including aluminium/Chromes/Anodized and alloys. This formulation is also effective and safe for use on all car surfaces and will not deteriorate clear coats. This preventative measure puts a stop to corrosion, IronX contains unique chemical ingredients that effectively dissolves the sintered iron by forming a water-soluble iron complex. No other method cleans paint and wheels as deeply as IronX.\n\nThe IronX Paint and wheels Decontamination System were developed as a method of removing paint contamination beyond what can be removed by washing or claying. If you are familiar with detail clay, you know it is capable of removing above surface contaminants that have bonded to the paint. The IronX is designed to remove what lies below the paint surface as well as above.\n\nAirborne chemical compounds and ferrous particles (particles containing iron) actually penetrate the paint and create corrosive compounds that eat deep into the paint's sub-layers or paint's pin-holes. This is a gradual process that often is not evident until it's too late. Claying does not remove the entire particle which will continue to spread beneath the surface if not dissolved.\n\nDuring the use of your vehicle, brake dust and road grime become sintered to the surface of the car paint, rims and wheels due to the high temperature conditions they are normally exposed. Brake dust contains high levels of iron and once sintered to the rim, becomes extremely difficult to dissolve or remove without the use of harsh chemicals. IronX opens up the paint's pores to release ferrous particles and to neutralize caustic compounds that have developed in the paint's subsurface. Ongoing damage is immediately stopped and future damage is prevented by removing the ferrous particles.\n\nIronX sprays on as a transparent liquid. As the cleansing liquid begins to work into the dirt and grime, the formula begins to turn purple/red. The purple/red coloration is the IronX Cleaner forming a bond to the sintered iron on the car paint and wheel and changing its state to a water soluble complex for easy removal. Stubborn, baked on grime may take a small amount of agitation. Rinse car paint and wheels thoroughly with a power washer and wipe dry.\n\nThe IronX is used by body shops for pre-cleaning prior to detailing and by dealerships for new and used car prep. It is proven to deliver a clean, glassy smooth vehicle that is protected from the harmful effects of paint contamination. No other is as fast and effective at removing multi-layer paint and wheels contamination.\n\nFeatures:\n- Removes Iron Particles and prevents the spread of iron-related damage & helps to protect your vehicle from paint system failure.\n- New Formula combines Cherry perfume to aid in masking Iron Dissolving Chemicals\n- Safe to use, Acid Free, and pH neutral (pH 6-7).\n- Safe to use on Clear Coat Paint\n- Safe to use on Aluminum, Chrome, Anodized, Alloy, or Clear coated wheels.\n- Safe for use on all solid car surfaces and will not deteriorate clear coats. (Avoid using on Fabric Convertible tops.)\n\nHow do iron particles appear on your car surface and where? Iron particles are all around us, and of course on our cars after travelling through the environment. They can be made from your car braking, driving near other cars, big trucks, train rails, industrial zones etc. They adhere to the car surface and once they \"stick\" to your paint due to their sharp edges together with sunshine they start to bake into the soft car paint layer where they oxidize and rust.\n\nHow to prevent iron dust from etching your paint? It's almost impossible to prevent the irons to stick on the surface, but it has been proven that inorganic coatings (such as Cquartz CQUK) that have self-cleaning effects can reduce the quantity of iron that adheres to the surface.\n\nHow to remove iron particles from the surface? There are a few options. Clay bar is one of them however claying will remove most of the irons by shaving them, which leaves some underneath the surface where it cannot reach. Also, clay could possibly mar your paint with micro scratches together with the iron it catches. Another option is by oxalic acid solutions. Though it may remove iron you can't be sure it is safe on paint, which depends on dilution (low pH), and it's not safe to use for your own health and environment. The third option is by Iron X, a pH-neutral product, which reacts only with iron particles which it dissolves. IronX contains a specific chemical that reacts aggressively with iron... BUT and it's big but, this chemical is very unstable if not mixed in the right %, its sensitive to heat as well.\n\nWhy does it change colour? Iron X changes colour to red/purple when coming in contact with iron particles, this is due to chemical reaction between the chemicals and iron.\n\nWill Iron X stain chrome wheels or chrome trims? No, it's completely safe to use on any chrome wheels, trim, or bare aluminium wheels. There is only one condition: Do not let it dry under sunlight.\n\nWill Iron X discolor wheel weights? Yes, it will. Wheel weights are made from lead, Iron X will change the lead colour to green. However light agitation will recover the original colour.\n\nWill Iron X affect brake callipers? For most high-end callipers it will not affect them however we have heard from customers in the past that Iron X can affect the paint colour of low-quality acrylic painted callipers. For this reason, we advise you to be more careful not to spray on them.\n\nWill Iron X remove wax from car paint? Yes and no, if it's a highly organic oil type it will affect the wax properties. If it's a synthetic polymer sealant it won't affect it much. On Cquartz or other inorganic coatings it won't affect them at all. In fact, it is even recommended for use on them.\n\nDoes Iron X remove tar spots as well? No, Iron X reacts only with iron particles.\n\nIs Iron X safe to use on 3M films venture shields? Yes, there is no problem at all using it on clear bra's and others.\n\nWhy does it smell bad? This is the nature of the chemical used, you cannot avoid this. If it doesn't smell so strong it means it has very little effect on iron or is a very diluted or inferior formula. We do advise you to use a facemask and latex (or Nitrile) gloves while using Iron X.\n\nCan I leave Iron X to dry on the surface? Yes, you can leave Iron X on the surface to dry, but not under direct sunshine! However, I don't suggest you leave any chemical composition to dry.\n\nIron Remover or Clay?\nIron removers are not meant to replace clay barring but to complement it. Iron remover will eliminate the majority of iron contaminants, making clay barring safer. A clay bar will not pick up as much contaminants and grit, reducing the risk of scratching the paint.\n\nGreat for cracks and crevices\nIronX is also excellent for decontaminating hard-to-reach areas, cracks, and crevices. It's a must for removing iron from complex areas such as wheels, rotors, brake calipers, etc.\n\nWhere can I spray this on?\nYou can use CARPRO IronX on all exterior surfaces: PPF, plastics, glass, rubber trims, wheels, aluminum, painted surfaces, and metal surfaces.\n\nAnything I should be aware of?\nAlways use IronX on cool surfaces. The reason is, you don't want the product to evaporate before it can chemically react with the iron fillings to bleed them off. And you don't want the 'purple' to dry on the surface. It does have a 'funky' smell, but don't worry, it's not toxic.\n\nDifference between IronX Cherry and Lemon Scent?\nThey share the majority of base chemistry and have equal potency. The only difference is that 'Lemon Scent' has an even less intrusive smell.\n\nIs it safe on PPF, decals and films (matte/gloss)?\nYes, safe on all surfaces. Just don't let it dry on those surfaces.\n\nProduct Images:\n\n\n\n\n\n

### Detaylı Açıklama
FRA-BER KO IRON – Demir Tozu Sökücü & Jant / Kaporta Dekontaminasyon Jelii (1 : 1 Konsantre) – 4,54 L

FRA-BER KO IRON’UN FAYDALARI | Morlaşan Reaksiyon, Derin Demir Temizliği, Düşük Koku

FRA-BER KO IRON, fren balatası tozu, ray kirleri, endüstriyel partikül ve asit yağmuru kalıntılarını mor renkli görsel reaksiyon eşliğinde çözen konsantre jel formüllü demir sökücüdür. Dikey yüzeylerde akmadan tutunur, düşük sülfür kokulu kiraz aroması sayesinde atölye içinde konforlu çalışma sunar.

ANA ÖZELLİKLER | FRA-BER KO IRON Ürün Özellikleri

• Morlaşan Demir Reaksiyonu: Mikropartikül Fe²? ile temas ettiğinde mor-kızıl renge dönerek etkiyi gösterir.
• Jel Kıvam & Yüksek Tutuş: Kaporta, jant ve cam yüzeylerde akmadan uzun temas süresi sağlar.
• Düşük Koku + Kiraz Aroması: Geleneksel thiol kokusunu minimuma indirir.
• Multi-Surface: Alaşım/çelik jant, vernikli boya, pencere camı ve plastik kaplama ile uyumlu.
• Konsantre Ekonomi: Saf veya 1 : 2’ye kadar seyreltilebilir; 4,54 L bidon ? 9 L hazır ürün.

FRA-BER KO IRON İDEAL KULLANIM ALANLARI | Nerelerde Kullanılır?

• Jantlarda pişmiş fren tozu ve sinek siyahı giderme
• Kaporta demir partikül dekontaminasyonu (kil işlemi öncesi)
• Cam yüzeylerde ray tozu ve oksit lekesi çözme
• Seramik kaplama öncesi kimyasal demir arındırma adımı
• Filo, tren ve ağır vasıtaların ray-endüstriyel kir temizliği

FRA-BER KO IRON KULLANIM SENARYOLARI | En İyi Sonuçlar İçin

• Showroom Rötuşu: Hafif demir lekesini 1 : 2 seyrelterek hızlı mor reaksiyon & durulama.
• Derin Jant Detayı: Saf jel + detay fırçası › 5 dk bekleme › basınçlı suyla durulama.
• Kaporta Kil Öncesi: 1 : 1 seyreltme ile panel panel morlaşma + kil lubricasyonu azaltma.
• Maraton Fren Testi Sonrası: Ağır balata tozu birikiminde çift uygulama.

FRA-BER KO IRON NASIL KULLANILIR? | Uygulama Talimatları

1. Hazırlık: Yüzey serin ve kuru olmalı; doğrudan güneş altında çalışmayın.
2. Püskürtme: Şişeyi çalkalayın, hedef bölgeye homojen film olarak sıkın.
3. Reaksiyon: 2 – 5 dk mor renge dönene kadar bekleyin; kurumasına izin vermeyin.
4. Fırçalama (opsiyonel): İnatçı kirde yumuşak jant fırçası kullanın.
5. Durulama: Bol su veya yüksek basınçla tamamen arındırın.
6. Panel Panel İlerleyin: Kaporta dekontaminasyonunda akıntı izini önler.

UYARILAR VE DEPOLAMA

• Sıcak yüzeye uygulamayın, ürünü kurutmayın.
• Dökme demir fren kaliperlerine direkt temas ettirmeyin.
• Hassas/yenilenmiş jantta önce görünmeyen noktada test edin.
• Koruyucu eldiven & gözlük kullanın.
• 5 °C – 30 °C aralığında, kapak kapalı, donma ve aşırı sıcaktan koruyarak saklayın.

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Yüzey serin ve kuru olmalı; doğrudan güneş altında çalışmayın.
2. Şişeyi çalkalayın, hedef bölgeye homojen film olarak sıkın.
3. 2-5 dakika mor renge dönene kadar bekleyin; kurumasına izin vermeyin.
4. İnatçı kirde yumuşak jant fırçası kullanın.
5. Bol su veya yüksek basınçla tamamen arındırın.
6. Panel panel ilerleyin.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Profesyonel detay stüdyoları ve yıkamacılar için ekonomik paket. Jant, kaporta ve cam dekontaminasyonu, seramik kaplama öncesi hazırlık için kullanılır.

**S: Seyreltme oranı nedir?**
C: Ağır kir için saf, standart bakım için 1:1, hafif kir için 1:2 oranında seyreltilebilir.

**S: Kaç araç için yeterli?**
C: 1:1 seyreltmeyle yaklaşık 60 araç jant temizliği için yeterlidir.

Fra-Ber’in LEGA spreyi, alaşım jantlar ve lastik yanaklarında biriken fren tozu, yağ ve yol kirlerini hızla çözer, parlatır ve antioksidan film ile uzun süre temiz kalmalarını sağlar. ANA ÖZELLİKLER | FRA-BER LEGA Ürün Özellikleri

• Tüm Araç Türleri: Otomobil, SUV, ticari araç, motosiklet ve karavan jantlarında etkili.

FRA-BER LEGA İDEAL KULLANIM ALANLARI | Nerelerde Kullanılır?

FRA-BER LEGA KULLANIM SENARYOLARI | En İyi Sonuçlar İçin

• Fırçasız Temas: Jel köpüğü 2 dk bekletip yüksek basınçlı suyla durulayarak çiziksiz temizlik.
• Fırça Destekli Detay: İnce jant fırçası ile erişilmesi zor yerlere mekanik etki ekleme.

• Kış Sonu Bakım: Tuz ve metal partiküllerini çözerek pas oluşumunu önleme.

FRA-BER LEGA NASIL KULLANILIR? | Uygulama Talimatları

1. Soğuk ve Kuru Yüzey: Jant sıcak değilken uygulayın.
2. Püskürtme: Şişeyi çalkalayın, janta 15–20 cm mesafeden eşit yoğunlukta sıkın.
3. Bekleme: 1–2 dk ürünü yüzeyde bırakın; kurumasına izin vermeyin.
4. Opsiyonel Fırçalama: Orta sert fırça ile kirleri gevşetin.
5. Durulama: Tercihen yüksek basınçlı suyla üstten aşağı iyice durulayın.
6. Kontrol: Gerekirse adımı tekrarlayın; sonrasında jant ve lastiği kurulayıp dressing uygulayın.
Kullanım: Ürün saf olarak kullanılır; seyreltme gerekmez.

## MG PS Orta Sert Mavi Kil Hamuru (SKU: MGPS-2019KM)

**Barkod:** 8683492661663
**Fiyat:** 280,00 TL
**Kategori:** AKSESUAR > Kil Ürünleri > Kil Hamurları

### Kısa Açıklama
MG PS Orta Sert Mavi Kil Hamuru, araç yüzeyindeki hafif ila orta seviyedeki kirleri güvenle temizler. Boya koruma ve detailing işlemleri öncesi etkili temizlik sağlar. 100 gr'lık oto bakım clay bar.

### Detaylı Açıklama
MG PS Orta Sert Kil Hamuru, reçine, zift, endüstriyel metal tozu ve fren tozu gibi inatçı kirleticileri boyadan nazikçe “çekip alır”. Orta sert formülü, ince kilden daha güçlü fakat agresif kil kadar sert olmayan dengeli bir yapıya sahiptir. Bu sayede mikro çizik riskini minimuma indirerek yüzeyi polisaj, wax ya da seramik kaplama öncesi pürüzsüz hâle getirir.

Teknik Özellikler:
• Aşındırıcılık: Orta (Medium Duty)
• Net Ağırlık: 100 g
• Renk: Mavi
• Malzeme: Polibütilen reçine + elastomer
• Uyumlu Yüzeyler: Boyalı sac, vernik, cam, krom, alüminyum, şeffaf plastik
• Ömür: Ortalama 10–20 araç (kir seviyesine bağlı)
• Saklama: Streç film / kutu içinde, serin ve gölgede

Öne Çıkan Özellikler:
• Orta Sert Güç – İnce kilin alamadığı reçine, su lekesi, zift ve metal tozunu güvenle söker.
• Çok Yönlü Kullanım – Boya, cam, metal ve plastik yüzeylerde iz bırakmadan çalışır.
• Mikro Çizik Önleme – Doğru kaydırıcıyla kullanıldığında hologram riskini en aza indirir.
• Renk Kodlu “Mavi” – Topladığı kirleri görüp kili zamanında katlamanızı kolaylaştırır.
• Tek Parça 100 g – Yeterli yüzey alanı ve pratik kullanım sağlar.

Detaylı Kullanım ve Uygulama Rehberi:
1. Araç Yıkama
Aracı pH-nötr şampuanla yıkayıp durulayın; gevşek kirleri tamamen temizleyin.
2. Kaydırıcı Hazırlığı
GYEON Q²M Clay Lube REDEFINED veya özel kil kaydırıcısı kullanın.
3. Kil Uygulaması
o Kil hamurundan avuç içi kadar koparın, yoğurup disk hâline getirin.
o Çalışacağınız paneli bol kaydırıcıyla ıslatın.
o Kili hafif baskıyla ileri-geri hareketlerle kaydırın.
o Pütür hissi kaybolunca panel temizdir; mikrofiber bezle silin.
4. Kili Yenileme
Kir biriktikçe kili katlayıp temiz yüzeyi ortaya çıkarın.
5. Yüzeyi Koruma
İşlem bittikten sonra wax, sealant veya seramik kaplama uygulayın.
Not: Kil hamurunu düşürürseniz içine kum/tortu girebilir ve boyayı çizebilir. Güvenlik için atıp yeni parça kullanın.

Kullanım Senaryoları:
• Hızlı Pre-Wax Hazırlığı
10 dakikada pürüzsüz zemin oluşturarak wax’ın tutunmasını güçlendirir.
• Endüstriyel Toz & Su Lekesi Temizliği
Metal partikül ve sert su izlerini çizmeden söker.
• PPF / Seramik Kaplama Öncesi
Kaplama öncesi görünmez kalıntıları temizleyerek yüzeyi hazırlar.
• Bakım Yıkamalarında Kil
Her 10.000 km’de bir ipeksi yüzey yenilemesi sağlar.
• Polisaj Öncesi Hazırlık
Zımpara/ped tıkanmasını önler, yüksek parlaklık sağlar.

Önerilen Aksesuar & Tamamlayıcı Ürünler:
• GYEON Q²M Clay Lube REDEFINED – Kil sürecinde ideal kaydırıcı.
• GYEON Q²M PolishWipe EVO – Yüzeyi çizmeden kurulamak için.
• GYEON Q²M Iron REDEFINED – Metal parçacıkları çözmek için kil öncesi kimyasal destek.

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ):
• Kil boyaya zarar verir mi?
Doğru kaydırıcıyla kullanıldığında mikro çizik oluşturmaz; vernik için güvenlidir.
• Ne sıklıkla kullanmalıyım?
Ortalama her yağ değişiminde (yaklaşık 10.000 km) veya polisaj / kaplama öncesinde.
• Tek bar kaç araç temizler?
Kirlilik durumuna göre ortalama 2–3 araç; ağır kirli yüzey tek bar tüketebilir.
• Düştüğünde ne yapmalıyım?
Kil yere temas ederse içine kum girer; atıp yeni parça kullanmanız gerekir.
• Cam ve jantta kullanabilir miyim?
Evet, pürüzsüz cam ve cilalı metal yüzeylerde güvenle kullanılabilir.

MG PS Orta Sert Kil Hamuru, detay tutkunlarına hızlı, güvenilir ve pürüzsüz sonuçlar sunar. Aracınızın parlaklığını ortaya çıkarmak artık sadece birkaç “kil geçişi” kadar kolay!

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Aracı pH nötr şampuanla yıkayıp durulayın.
2. Kil kaydırıcısı hazırlayın (GYEON ClayLube önerilir).
3. Kil hamurundan avuç içi kadar koparın, yoğurup disk hâline getirin.
4. Çalışacağınız paneli bol kaydırıcıyla ıslatın.
5. Kili hafif baskıyla ileri-geri hareketlerle kaydırın.
6. Pütür hissi kaybolunca panel temizdir; mikrofiber bezle silin.
7. Kir biriktikçe kili katlayıp temiz yüzeyi ortaya çıkarın.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Hızlı wax hazırlığı, endüstriyel toz ve su lekesi temizliği, PPF/seramik kaplama öncesi, bakım yıkamalarında, polisaj öncesi hazırlık için kullanılır.

• Mikro çizik önleme - hologram riskini azaltır
• Renk kodlu mavi - topladığı kirleri görmenizi sağlar
• 100 gr - 10-20 araç için yeterli

### Kısa Açıklama
MG PS Agresif Yüzey Temizleyici Mor Kil Hamuru, araç yüzeyindeki zift, reçine ve endüstriyel kirleri etkili şekilde temizler. Boya koruma ve detaylı temizlik için ideal 100 gr’lık güçlü clay bar.

### Detaylı Açıklama
Fabrikasyon boya kalıntıları, kalın zift birikintileri, fren balata demir tozu katmanları ve sanayi kirleri… Standart veya orta sertlikteki kil hamurlarının zorlandığı kirleticiler için özel olarak geliştirildi.

MG PS Agresif Yüzey Temizleyici Kil Hamuru, mor renkli ve yüksek aşındırıcılı polibütilen reçine + elastomer bileşimi sayesinde boyaya gömülmüş partikülleri güvenle “çekip alır” ve yüzeyi polisaja hazır hâle getirir.

Not: Yüksek temizlik gücü nedeniyle mikro matlık bırakabilir; uygulama sonrası hafif bir polisaj tavsiye edilir. Profesyonel detaycılar ve ileri seviye kullanıcılar için uygundur.

Teknik Özellikler:
• Aşındırıcılık: Yüksek (Heavy Duty)
• Net Ağırlık: 100 g
• Renk: Mor
• Malzeme: Polibütilen reçine + elastomer
• Uyumlu Yüzeyler: Boyalı sac, vernik, cam, krom, alüminyum
• Dayanım: 10–20 araç (kir seviyesine bağlı)
• Saklama: Streç film / kutu içinde, serin ve gölgede

Kullanım Talimatı:
1. Ön Yıkama
Aracı pH-nötr şampuanla yıkayıp durulayın.
2. Kaydırıcı Uygulaması
Bol miktarda kil kaydırıcısı veya detay spreyi sıkın. (GYEON Q²M Clay Lube önerilir.)
3. Kil Hazırlığı
100 g’lık barın yarısını koparıp yoğurun ve disk hâline getirin.
4. Kil İşlemi
o Kili hafif baskıyla ileri-geri ve çapraz hareketlerle kaydırın.
o Direnç azaldığında panel temizlenmiş demektir.
o Kir toplandıkça kili katlayıp temiz yüzeyi ortaya çıkarın.
5. Silme & Kontrol
Mikrofiber bezle paneli kurulayın; gerekirse işlemi tekrarlayın.
6. Yüzey Finishi
Hafif polisaj + koruyucu wax veya seramik kaplama ile parlaklığı mühürleyin.
Güvenlik İpucu: Kil yere düşerse içine kum girebilir; çizik riskine karşı mutlaka atıp yeni parça kullanın.

Kullanım Senaryoları:
• Polisaj Öncesi Derin Temizlik
Zımpara ve pad tıkanmasını önler, daha yüksek parlaklık elde edilmesini sağlar.
• Boya Overspray & Zift Temizliği
Boya sisleri ve kalın zift katmanlarını hızla söker.
• Endüstriyel Fallout Giderme
Metal partikülleri kimyasal + mekanik kombinasyonla temizler.
• PPF / Seramik Kaplama Hazırlığı
Kaplamanın tutunacağı pürüzsüz bir alt zemin oluşturur.

Önerilen Aksesuarlar:

• GYEON Q²M PolishWipe EVO – Mikro-marring riski olmadan kalıntıları siler.

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular (FAQ):

Agresif kil, daha sert ve kalın kirlerde etkilidir; mikro matlık bırakabilir, ardından hafif polisaj önerilir.

Doğru kaydırıcıyla kullanıldığında güvenlidir; ancak hafif marring bırakabilir.

• Kil düştüğünde ne yapmalıyım?
Yüzeye kum yapışacağı için mutlaka atıp yeni parça kullanın.

Sadece püskürt ve kurumuş böcek lekelerini anında çöz! Ön yıkama şampuanı + organik solvent hibrit formülü, sinek kalıntıları ile ağır yol kirini tek adımda söker; seramik kaplama, wax ve plastiklerde tam uyum sağlar.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

> Hızlı Böcek Çözme — Kurumuş sinek, böcek ve reçine artığını 1-2 dk’da eritir.
> Hibrit Güç — Şampuan bazlı deterjan + solvent karışımıyla 8,5 / 10 temizlik.
> Fırçasız Temizlik — Agresif ovmaya gerek kalmaz, çizik riski yok.
> Kaplama & Wax Dostu — Seramik kaplamayı, cila ve wax’ı bozmaz.
> Çok Yönlü Uyum — Boya, cam, plastik trim, metal ve lastikte güvenle kullanılır.
> Kullanıma Hazır — Seyreltme gerekmez; zamandan tasarruf sağlar.

Nasıl Kullanılır?

3. Durulama – Basınçlı suyla yukarıdan aşağıya iyice yıkayın.
4. Fırçalama (Opsiyonel) – Amblem, kapı içi gibi zorlu bölgelerde yumuşak fırça kullanın.
5. Kontrol – Kalıntı kaldıysa adımları tekrarlayın.

• Motorsport & Rally Artıkları — Yüksek hızda biriken kauçuk ve film kirini söker.

# Q²M BUG&GRIME

## Exterior / maintenance

### Dedicated pre wash cleaner for insects and road grime.

Q²M Bug & Grime is a strong and efficient pre-wash product designed to quickly and safely remove insects and road grime. It effectively dissolves contamination, allowing for a safer and easier wash process afterwards. The formula works fast and is safe for use on coated surfaces.

-

## Strong and effective bug and grime remover.

Q²M Bug & Grime simplifies the removal of stubborn insect residue and heavy grime that regular shampoos struggle with. It prepares the surface for washing and helps reduce the risk of scratches during the main wash stage.

Features:
- EASY BUG REMOVAL
- HIGHLY CONCENTRATED
- SUITABLE ON ALL SURFACES

## TECHNICAL DETAILS

CAPACITIES: 500 ML / 1000 ML / 4000 ML
COATING SAFE: yes
PH LEVEL: 11
Consumption: 80-150ml / car

## HOW TO USE

01. Spray Q²M Bug & Grime onto affected areas.
02. Allow the product to dwell briefly without drying.
03. Rinse thoroughly with a pressure washer.
04. Repeat or agitate gently if needed.
05. Continue with the regular wash process.

## FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS

Is Q²M Bug & Grime safe for ceramic coatings?
Yes. It is safe for coated and uncoated surfaces. Bear in mind excessive use may impact the hydrophobic properties of a coating.

Can it remove old insect residue?
As long as it is not etched in the clearcoat, yes.

Does it require agitation?
Usually no, but light agitation can help with heavy contamination.

Can it be used on all exterior surfaces?
Yes. It is safe for typical exterior vehicle surfaces.

## Description

Gyeon Q²M Bug & Grime remover is a highly effective but safe product for removing tough stains on paintwork such as general road grime and squashed insects.

Are you tired of battling unsightly bug splatters, stubborn tar spots, and baked-on road grime? Gyeon Bug & Grime is your secret weapon for effortlessly dissolving these persistent contaminants before your main wash, ensuring a truly deep clean and a flawless shine.

### Why Choose Gyeon Bug & Grime?

- **Powerful Yet Safe Formula:** Engineered to effectively break down and lift organic and inorganic contaminants like insect remains, tree sap, bird droppings, and general road film, without damaging your vehicle's paint, trim, or protective coatings.
- **Pre-Wash Essential:** Applied before your main shampoo, Bug & Grime drastically reduces the risk of scratching your paintwork during the wash process by encapsulating and lifting away the most aggressive debris.
- **Effortless Application:** Simply spray onto the affected areas, allow it to dwell for a few minutes, and rinse away. No harsh scrubbing required!
- **Pleasant Citrus Scent:** Enjoy a fresh burst of citrus while you detail, transforming a chore into a more enjoyable experience.
- **Economical and Effective:** A little goes a long way. It's concentrated formula ensures excellent value for money.
- **Trusted Gyeon Quality:** From the innovators behind world-renowned ceramic coatings, Gyeon Bug & Grime embodies the same commitment to quality, performance, and user experience.

### How Gyeon Bug & Grime Works:

Bug & Grime's advanced chemical formulation penetrates and emulsifies stubborn organic and inorganic contaminants. It loosens their grip on your vehicle's surface, making them easy to rinse away, preventing them from being spread and potentially scratched into your paintwork during a traditional wash.

### Gyeon Bug & Grime is perfect for:

- **Removing Insect Remains:** The bane of summer driving, effectively dissolved and removed.
- **Tackling Tree Sap:** Effortlessly lifts sticky tree sap, pollen, and other organic residues.
- **Dissolving Bird Droppings:** Quickly and safely removes aggressive bird droppings before they etch your paint.
- **Pre-Wash Degreasing:** Gently loosens and removes road film, light tar, and general grime.
- **Maintaining Ceramic Coatings & Waxes:** Safe to use on vehicles protected with sealants, waxes, and ceramic coatings.

### How to Use:

- Ensure the surface is cool to the touch.
- Shake the bottle well. Spray Gyeon Bug & Grime liberally onto dry exterior surfaces of your vehicle, paying close attention to areas with heavy bug splatter or grime accumulation.
- Allow the product to dwell for 2-5 minutes (do not let it dry on the surface).
- Rinse thoroughly with a pressure washer or hose.
- Proceed with your regular Gyeon Bathe Shampoo and the two-bucket wash method.

**Pro Tip:** For extremely stubborn, baked-on insects, you can gently agitate the product with a soft detailing brush or wash mitt after the dwell time, before rinsing.

Available in 400ml, 1 Litre & 4 Litre Bottles

### Product Description

Gyeon Bug & Grime helps you remove bug smear and road grime fast and easy. We have all had the experience where bugs just keep splattering on your windshield and impair your vision. If you are lucky your windshield wipers and washer fluid can remove most of the bug smear. Best case scenario your glass is relatively clean but what about the rest of your vehicle? If the bugs are hitting your windshield, you can bet they are hitting your bumper and the front of your hood as well. The guts of these bugs are often very acidic and it is important to remove them from the paint and sensitive surfaces asap. The longer you let them sit on the surface, the deeper they can etch into the surface, adding imperfections that need to be polished away. With Gyeon Bug & Grime, you can simply spray the surface, let it dwell and rinse away or agitate with your wash mitt. The application is that easy and the strong formula will help break down and loosen the guts for easy and safe removal. Bug & Grime works great on bugs, but you can also use it to help remove road grime, dirt, tar, and other nasty road contamination. Don't let bug guts stick to your paint, remove them with the Gyeon Bug & Grime!

### From The Label

Removes bugs and grime in an instant!

- Easy bug removal
- Highly concentrated
- Safe on all surfaces

### Directions

Spray a moderate amount directly on the surface. Leave up to 2 minutes to soften the contamination. Rinse with a pressure washer. Do not use on hot paint or in direct sunlight. Do not dry on paint or trim. KEEP OUT OF REACH OF CHILDREN.

Reviewed by Cameron P. on 4/3/2017 (DI Verified Purchase)
Would they buy this item again? No
Bought this to try out some of Gyeon's products. While the product works, it doesn't work as well as it should. Initial use seemed promising, as it softened some of the harder road splatter, and removed bug carcasses. But, it certainly was not as effortless as the packaging reads- I still had to clay to remove a lot of the crud that had piled up, even after letting it dwell. It smells like a standard degreaser too- so I figure save your money and buy something like Tar-X or use an APC if you're not concerned about your underlying wax or coating. I'm wondering if this product is mainly designed for cars that are coated. While mine had a layer of Hydr02 on it when I used the product, perhaps it's more suited for something that has a legitimate Si coating on it, like Gyeon Q2 or CarPro's CQuartz. I cannot test this as I have neither on my car at the moment.

### FAQ

Where can I use Bug & Grime remover, and are there any precautions?
Bug & Grime can be used on delicate finishes such as PPF, wraps, rubber and textured plastics without causing harm. It can be sprayed on the entire vehicle, including wheels and wheel wells, before snow foam for a deep pre-soak clean.

Will it take off my waxes?
It likely won't take it off right away, but be mindful that any chemicals will affect waxes and sealants in some way. But Bug & Grime is safe on coating.

Can I use it as a adhesive and tree sap remover?
No, use GYEON Tar (solvent-based) for that.

Does it effectively remove traffic film?
It helps, but most of the time, you'll need to do a contact wash or use GYEON Traffic Film Remover.

## How to Use

### Step 1: Pre-Wash Your Vehicle
Before using the Gyeon Q2M Bug & Grime Remover, pre-wash your vehicle with water to remove any loose dirt and debris. This will help ensure that the solution is able to penetrate and break down the tougher contaminants.

### Step 2: Spray the Solution
Spray the Gyeon Q2M Bug & Grime Remover directly onto the surface you will be working on. Be sure to cover the entire area thoroughly, especially any areas with heavy bug or grime buildup.

### Step 3: Allow to Dwell
Allow the solution to dwell on the surface for 3-5 minutes, depending on the severity of the contamination. This will allow the solution to penetrate and break down the bugs and grime, making them easier to remove.

### Step 4: Agitate with a Microfiber Towel
Using a high-quality microfiber towel, agitate the surface gently in a circular motion. This will help to loosen and remove the bugs and grime from the surface.

### Step 5: Rinse Thoroughly
Rinse the surface thoroughly with water to remove any remaining solution and contaminants. Use a pressure washer if possible to ensure a thorough rinse.

### Step 6: Dry the Surface
Dry the surface using a clean microfiber towel or a blower. This will help to prevent water spots from forming on the surface.

## PH Neutral Tar Remover

Unlike most tar removers, Gyeon Tar does not impact any exterior surfaces and is safe for bodywork. It is suitable for use on paint, glass, and plastic trim (both painted and unpainted). Being pH neutral, it can also be used to remove tar spots from bare polished lips or ceramic-coated vehicles.

## Efficient & Safe

Over time, vehicles tend to accumulate significant amounts of tar and road contamination. Gyeon Tar expedites the decontamination process by dissolving the majority of tar and contaminants, making your claying process easier and safer. Fewer contaminants result in a reduced chance of marring the paint.

## Remove Adhesive and Tar

Gyeon Tar is exceptionally effective in removing adhesive residues, efficiently dissolving organic contaminants and glues. Work on one panel at a time, ensuring the product does not dry on the surface. Be extra cautious when working on PPF (recommended 30 seconds dwell time only).

TIP: Prepare a bucket with hot water and use a soaked Q²M SilkMitt to enhance contamination removal. Wash the car once the work is completed.

## FAQ

Q: Can I use Iron Remover at the same time?
A: Yes, use Iron first, wash it off, then apply Tar. After Tar, use soap for a final wash.

Q: How to use it?
A: Ensure the panel is cool. Work on a small section at a time, do not let the product dry, then rinse off.

Q: Can I apply it on PPF?
A: Certainly, exercise caution. Work on a cool, small section at a time, and ensure not to let it sit for longer than 30 seconds. Rinse off thoroughly with soap afterward. Repeat the process if needed.

Q: Will Gyeon Tar damage my trim/paint/coating?
A: No, it wouldn't, as long as the product does not dry out and is rinsed off thoroughly.

Q: Is Gyeon Tar safe on Deco?
A: We recommend avoiding spraying it on decorations. If you accidentally spray some on, rinse it off immediately.

Q: Spray trigger not working after use?
A: It is a solvent product, so there's a high chance it will damage the trigger. We recommend removing the sprayer, rinsing it, and putting the cap back on after use.

## GYEON Q²M TAR REDEFINED

What's so special about Q²M Tar REDEFINED?

Q²M Tar Redefined is a tar remover that won't damage exterior surfaces and is safe for bodywork. It can be used safely on paint, glass, and plastic trim, both painted and unpainted. Thanks to its pH-neutral formula, it's even suitable for removing tar stains from bare, polished lips without damage.

### Safely speeds up the detailing process

With daily use, a vehicle quickly accumulates tar and asphalt contaminants, especially on high-powered vehicles with aggressive driving. Q²M Tar Redefined offers an excellent solution to this problem. Its LOW VOC formula accelerates the decontamination process and minimizes time-consuming steps like claying. It's a healthier product for the user and ensures that contaminants are quickly dissolved, allowing you to achieve a smooth finish in record time.

### The REDEFINED line

With the REDEFINED line, GYEON has taken its renowned chemical formulas to a whole new level. By reworking and refining them, we deliver unparalleled performance, exceptional durability, and ease of use, ensuring our customers have the best possible experience.

### Best practices and pro tips from Yves Heylen

Q²M Tar Redefined is not only a tar remover, but also effectively dissolves organic contaminants and adhesive residue. Work panel by panel to prevent the product from drying out. TIP: Prepare a bucket of hot water and use a soaked Q²M SilkMitt to remove contaminants more effectively. Wash the car thoroughly after completing the work.

## MANUAL

How do you use Q²M Tar REDEFINED?

Q²M Tar is not only a tar remover, but also effectively dissolves organic contamination or adhesives. Work panel by panel, preventing the product from drying out.

TIP: Prepare a bucket of hot water and use a soaked Q²M SilkMitt to remove dirt more effectively. Wash the car once the process is complete.

## Product Information

## Product Description

Gyeon Tar is a gentle, yet strong tar remover! Tar and other contamination is a real problem for almost any vehicle. With all of the road grime, dirt, etc. that comes into contact with the exterior of your vehicle when driving, it is no wonder that a simple shampoo can not always do the job. When you have tar and other embedded contamination, a stronger formula is needed. This is where Gyeon Tar comes into play! When sprayed onto the surface, this high end formula will target and dissolve hard to remove tar. This not only helps clean the area but speeds up the whole decontamination process. Tar is pH neutral and safe on most surfaces including paint, glass, most rims, and trim, leaving it smooth and ready for the next step in the detailing process. If you have any extra stubborn tar build ups, Gyeon recommends a second application and/or agitating the tar with a wash mitt or a clay bar. Once finished, rinse and wash the panel Tar was used on thoroughly to reveal a squeaky clean shine! When you are looking to remove stubborn tar, grab a bottle of Gyeon Tar to get the job done!

## Professional Detailer Reviews

The main application for Gyeon Q2M Tar is pretty self explanatory. It is used to safely remove tar and rubber from a good day at the track, tree sap on paint, or as a chemical decontamination when you don't want to introduce a clay bar. Q2M Tar is extremely safe and ph neutral. It can be used on paint, plastic trim, glass, even polished wheels without worry.

## From The Label

### Product Description

Removes tar and organic sediments effectively and safely. Does not affect coatings. Easily removes adhesives and glue.

- Low voc content
- Easy removal of contamination
- Safe on all surfaces

### Directions

Use after Q2M Iron for full surface decontamination. Wash the car with a HQ, pH neutral shampoo. Rinse well and dry. Spray onto the panel, wait for approx. 1-2 minutes and wipe carefully with a Q2M SilkMitt Evo. Wash the car with a bodywork shampoo afterwards. Possible use on paint, plastic or any other exterior surface including wheels. KEEP OUT OF REACH OF CHILDREN.

## Product Description

Remove tar without the hassle!

GYEON Tar provides is an easy-to-use tar remover that quickly and gently dissolves tar from vehicle surfaces. This strong formula is powerful enough to remove tar, sap, and other stubborn contaminants, yet it's safe enough to use on paintwork, glass, and even painted and unpainted plastics. GYEON Tar helps you decontaminate an entire vehicle in a fraction of the time that it would take to use detailing clay.

If you drive a high-performance vehicle, you're no stranger to tar. It's a general rule that, the higher the horsepower, the more aggressively a car is driven. When a car is driven hard, there will be tar! GYEON Tar makes removing tar easier than ever before, by simply dissolving it so that it can be rinsed away!

GYEON Tar is faster than clay, and it's also gentler. If your vehicle has soft paint, even a soft microfiber towel can cause marring, so imagine rubbing a clay bar all over the paint! GYEON Tar eliminates the risk of marring paint with clay. Even if your vehicle doesn't have soft paint, you'll appreciate the speed and efficiency of removing tar and other contaminants with GYEON Tar.

## How to Use

Work on a cool surface out of direct sunlight.

1. Wash and rinse the vehicle thoroughly.
2. Spray a liberal amount of GYEON Tar onto the affected area.
3. Allow to dwell for 2-4 minutes. DO NOT ALLOW GYEON TAR TO DRY ON THE SURFACE.
4. Use a damp microfiber towel to wipe away any stubborn areas.
5. Rinse the vehicle thoroughly.

Size: 500 ml

## Bugs and traffic film
Q²M Bug&Grime is a strong and highly efficient pre-wash product developed specifically for the removal of insects, bugs, and grime. It dissolves contamination and ensures a safe and scratch-free wash afterward. It is the first-choice product after every summer evening ride. Q²M Bug&Grime works quickly and effectively while being coating-safe at the same time.

Dissolves soil and coating-safe.
Q²M Bug&Grime can be used as a strong and effective pre-spray during the initial steps of a thorough wash. Simply leave it on the surface and then rinse it off. It's also a fantastic aid during a more intensive cleaning process and will remove old and heavily settled dirt when agitated with a gentle brush.

## GYEON Bug & Grime

### Superb maintenance products for outstanding detailing performance

Q²M Bug & Grime is a strong and very efficient pre-wash product, that has been developed specially for the removal of insects, bugs and grime. It dissolves contamination and ensures a safe and scratch-free wash afterwards. It's the first choice product after every summer-evening ride. Q²M Bug&Grime works fast and effective and is wax-safe at the same time.

- CONSUMPTION: 80-150ml / car
- PH LEVEL: 9
- COATING SAFE: yes

### STRONG & READY TO USE

Q²M Bug&Grime can be used as a strong and effective pre-spray during the first steps of a thorough wash, leaving it on the surface and rinsing it off. At the same time, it's a fantastic aid during a more intensive cleaning process and will remove old and heavily settled dirt while agitated with a gentle brush.

### THE ULTIMATE BUG&GRIME REMOVER

Q²M Bug & Grime is a strong, ready-to-use product, that has been developed to dissolve insects, bugs and road grime stains in a fast and safe way. Just a single application and rinsing with an effective pressure washer will remove most of the visible contamination, even old and resistant stains. Despite its strength, Q²M Bug&Grime is safe for all types of paintwork, quartz coatings and most waxes!

### ADVICE ON MAINTENANCE

Spray a moderate amount directly on the surface. Leave to soften the contamination. Rinse with a pressure washer and a large amount of water. DO NOT use on hot paint or in direct sunlight. Do not dry on paintwork or trim. The product is also environmentally friendly.

Strong & safe
Q²M Bug&Grime is a strong, ready-to-use product developed to dissolve insects, bugs, and road grime stains quickly and safely. A single application and rinsing with an effective pressure washer will remove most visible contamination, even old and resistant stains. Despite its strength, Q²M Bug&Grime is safe for all types of paintwork, ceramic coatings and PPF.
TIP: Use only on cold paint, never in direct sunlight, or on a warm car. Do not let the product dry.

### FAQ

Where can I use Bug & Grime remover, and are there any precautions?
Bug & Grime can be used on delicate finishes such as PPF, wraps, rubber and textured plastics without causing harm. It can be sprayed on the entire vehicle, including wheels and wheel wells, before snow foam for a deep pre-soak clean.

Will it take off my waxes?
It likely won't take it off right away, but be mindful that any chemicals will affect waxes and sealants in some way. But Bug & Grime is safe on coating.

Can I use it as a adhesive and tree sap remover?
No, use GYEON Tar (solvent-based) for that.

Does it effectively remove traffic film?
It helps, but most of the time, you'll need to do a contact wash or use GYEON Traffic Film Remover.

> Kaynak 2: https://www.prodetailingsupplies.ca/product-page/gyeon-q-m-bug-grime-remover

## Description

Gyeon Q²M Bug & Grime remover is a highly effective but safe product for removing tough stains on paintwork such as general road grime and squashed insects.

Are you tired of battling unsightly bug splatters, stubborn tar spots, and baked-on road grime? Gyeon Bug & Grime is your secret weapon for effortlessly dissolving these persistent contaminants before your main wash, ensuring a truly deep clean and a flawless shine.

### Why Choose Gyeon Bug & Grime?

- **Powerful Yet Safe Formula:** Engineered to effectively break down and lift organic and inorganic contaminants like insect remains, tree sap, bird droppings, and general road film, without damaging your vehicle's paint, trim, or protective coatings.
- **Pre-Wash Essential:** Applied before your main shampoo, Bug & Grime drastically reduces the risk of scratching your paintwork during the wash process by encapsulating and lifting away the most aggressive debris.
- **Effortless Application:** Simply spray onto the affected areas, allow it to dwell for a few minutes, and rinse away. No harsh scrubbing required!
- **Pleasant Citrus Scent:** Enjoy a fresh burst of citrus while you detail, transforming a chore into a more enjoyable experience.
- **Economical and Effective:** A little goes a long way. It's concentrated formula ensures excellent value for money.
- **Trusted Gyeon Quality:** From the innovators behind world-renowned ceramic coatings, Gyeon Bug & Grime embodies the same commitment to quality, performance, and user experience.

### How Gyeon Bug & Grime Works:

Bug & Grime's advanced chemical formulation penetrates and emulsifies stubborn organic and inorganic contaminants. It loosens their grip on your vehicle's surface, making them easy to rinse away, preventing them from being spread and potentially scratched into your paintwork during a traditional wash.

### Gyeon Bug & Grime is perfect for:

- **Removing Insect Remains:** The bane of summer driving, effectively dissolved and removed.
- **Tackling Tree Sap:** Effortlessly lifts sticky tree sap, pollen, and other organic residues.
- **Dissolving Bird Droppings:** Quickly and safely removes aggressive bird droppings before they etch your paint.
- **Pre-Wash Degreasing:** Gently loosens and removes road film, light tar, and general grime.
- **Maintaining Ceramic Coatings & Waxes:** Safe to use on vehicles protected with sealants, waxes, and ceramic coatings.

### How to Use:

- Ensure the surface is cool to the touch.
- Shake the bottle well. Spray Gyeon Bug & Grime liberally onto dry exterior surfaces of your vehicle, paying close attention to areas with heavy bug splatter or grime accumulation.
- Allow the product to dwell for 2-5 minutes (do not let it dry on the surface).
- Rinse thoroughly with a pressure washer or hose.
- Proceed with your regular Gyeon Bathe Shampoo and the two-bucket wash method.

**Pro Tip:** For extremely stubborn, baked-on insects, you can gently agitate the product with a soft detailing brush or wash mitt after the dwell time, before rinsing.

Available in 400ml, 1 Litre & 4 Litre Bottles

INNOVACAR D3 TAR Zift, Reçine, Yapışkan Kalıntı Temizleyici – 500 ml

INNOVACAR D3 TAR’IN FAYDALARI | Güçlü Zift Çözme, Yüzey Güvenliğiyle Birlikte

Innovacar D3 TAR, araç kaportasında biriken zift, reçine, yapışkan ve asfalt kalıntılarını etkili şekilde çözen, aynı zamanda yüzeye zarar vermeyen özel bir dekontaminasyon ürünüdür. Klasik solvent bazlı temizleyicilerin aksine petrol damıtığı içermez, böylece hem çevreye hem de korumalı yüzeylere karşı daha güvenlidir.
• Zift ve Asfalt Çözücü: Yol birikintileri, zift lekeleri, asfalt kalıntılarını çözer ve tamamen temizler.
• Reçine ve Yapışkan Temizleyici: Ağaç reçineleri, etiket yapışkanları, film/folyo artıkları için uygundur.
• Yavaş Buharlaşma: Su bazlı formülü sayesinde ürün yüzeyde uzun süre kalır, derinlemesine etki gösterir.
• Yüzeye Dost Yapı: Mevcut seramik kaplamalara zarar vermez, kaplama öncesi yüzey hazırlığı için uygundur.
• Solvent İçermez: EDTA, NTA, fosfat ve petrol damıtığı içermez. Çevre ve kullanıcı dostudur.

Hacim: 500 ml
Ortalama Tüketim: 100 ml / araç
pH: Nötr (ürün bilgilerine göre değerlendirilmiştir)

ANA ÖZELLİKLER | D3 TAR Ürün Özellikleri

• Zift, reçine, yapışkan çözücü etkili temizleyici
• Su bazlı, yavaş buharlaşan formül
• Solvent içermez, yüzeye naziktir
• Boya, cam, plastik gibi hassas yüzeylerle uyumludur
• Seramik kaplama öncesi uygulamalar için ideal yüzey hazırlığı sağlar
• Etiket, film, PPF yapışkanı kalıntılarının temizliğinde uygundur

D3 TAR İDEAL KULLANIM ALANLARI | Nerelerde Kullanılır?

• Kaporta üzerindeki zift, asfalt, reçine ve sinek kalıntıları
• Cam yüzeylerde reçine, bant ve film kalıntıları
• Etiket, sticker, folyo sökümleri sonrası yapışkan artıkları
• Jant kenarları, marşpiyel altı, çamurluk içleri
• Kaplama öncesi detaylı yüzey hazırlığı süreçlerinde

D3 TAR NASIL KULLANILIR? | Uygulama Talimatları

1. Ürünü seyreltilmeden (saf) kullanın.
2. İşlem yapılacak yüzeyin soğuk ve gölgede olduğundan emin olun.
3. Ürünü doğrudan ziftli veya kirli yüzeye püskürtün.
4. 2–5 dakika arası reaksiyon süresi tanıyın. Kurumasına izin vermeyin.
5. Yumuşak mikrofiber bezle kalıntıyı silin veya bol su ile durulayın.
6. Gerekirse, inatçı kalıntılarda işlemi tekrarlayın.

UYARILAR
• Ürünü sıcak yüzeylere uygulamayın.
• Uygulama sonrası kurumasına izin vermeyin.
• PPF, vinil film, yeni boyanmış yüzeyler veya rötuşlanmış alanlarda kullanmadan önce küçük bir bölgede test edin.
• Ürünü panel bazında uygulayın.
• Göz ile temasından kaçının.

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Ürünü seyreltilmeden (saf) kullanın.
2. İşlem yapılacak yüzeyin soğuk ve gölgede olduğundan emin olun.
3. Ürünü doğrudan ziftli veya kirli yüzeye püskürtün.
4. 2-5 dakika reaksiyon süresi tanıyın; kurumasına izin vermeyin.
5. Yumuşak mikrofiber bezle kalıntıyı silin veya bol su ile durulayın.
6. İnatçı kalıntılarda işlemi tekrarlayın.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Kaporta üzerindeki zift, asfalt ve reçine kalıntıları, cam yüzeylerde bant ve film kalıntıları, etiket/sticker/folyo sökümü sonrası yapışkan artıkları için kullanılır.

### Hedef Yüzeyler
Boya, cam, plastik

### Neden Bu Ürün?
• Solvent içermez - yüzeye nazik
• Su bazlı - yavaş buharlaşan formül
• Seramik kaplama öncesi ideal yüzey hazırlığı
• EDTA/NTA ve fosfat içermez

### İlişkili Ürünler
- **Alternatifler:** GYEON QM Tar REDEFINED (Q2M-TR500M), GYEON QM Tar REDEFINED (Q2M-TR1000M)

### Sıkça Sorulan Sorular
**S: Solvent içeriyor mu?**
C: Hayır, petrol damıtığı içermeyen su bazlı formüldür; çevreye ve korumalı yüzeylere daha güvenlidir.

**S: PPF üzerinde kullanılabilir mi?**
C: Kullanmadan önce küçük bir bölgede test edin; yeni veya hassas PPF'lerde dikkatli olun.

## GYEON QM WaterSpot (SKU: Q2M-WSYA1000M)

**Barkod:** 8683492661434
**Fiyat:** 830,00 TL
**Kategori:** DIŞ YÜZEY > Yüzey Hazırlık ve Temizleyiciler > Boyalı Yüzey Temizleyiciler

### Kısa Açıklama
GYEON QM WaterSpot, su lekesi giderici ve kireç çözücü, 1000 ml. MTS Kimya güvencesiyle orijinal ürün.

### Detaylı Açıklama
GYEON Q²M WaterSpot Kireç Çözücü Cam Su Lekesi Temizleyici Çıkarıcı – 1000 ml

Sadece püskürt ve kireç lekelerini saniyeler içinde sil! pH 2 asidik formülü, boya ve cam yüzeylerdeki mineral birikintilerini hızla çözer; seramik kaplamalarda dahi matlaşma bırakmaz.

Öne Çıkan Özellikler

> Hızlı Leke Çözme — 30 sn içinde su lekesi & kireci eritir.
> Seramik Kaplama Dostu — Kaplamayı bozmaz, parlaklığı geri kazandırır.
> Yüksek Temizlik Gücü — pH 2 asidik yapı 10/10 etki sunar.
> Çok Yönlü Kullanım — Boya, cam, plastik, krom ve trimlerde iz bırakmaz.
> Pasta Gerektirmez — Yeni lekeleri zımpara / polisaj olmadan yok eder.
> Kolay Uygulama — Sprey + mikrofiber; panel panel hızla ilerleyin.

Teknik Bilgiler

Parametre Değer Not
Tüketim 25 ml/araç Ortalama sedan
pH Seviyesi 2 (asidik) Fosforik asit bazlı
Etki Süresi ? 30 sn Kurumadan sil
Kullanıma Hazır Evet Seyreltilmez
Çalışma Sıcaklığı 5 – 30 °C Gölge tavsiye
Ambalaj 1000 ml Püskürtme başlıklı

Nasıl Kullanılır?

1. Hazırlık – Araç temiz & kuru olmalı.
2. Püskürtme – 15-20 cm mesafeden lekeye sıkın; panel panel çalışın.
3. Bekleme – Maks. 30 sn; ürünün kurumasına izin vermeyin.
4. Silme – Yumuşak mikrofiberle tek yönlü silin.
5. Durulama – Duru suyla kalıntıları tamamen uzaklaştırın.
6. Tekrar – İnatçı lekede adımları yenileyin.

Kullanım Alanları

• Yıkama Sonrası Su Lekesi Silme — Güneşte kuruyan damlaları dakikada yok eder.
• Kaplama Bakımı — İlk haftalardaki lekeleri kaplamaya zarar vermeden temizler.
• Cam & Ayna Kireç Çözme — Cam tavan ve aynalarda kristal berraklık sağlar.
• Sert Su Bölgesi Bakımı — Kapı altı ve pencere kenarındaki kireç halkalarını giderir.
• Krom & Metal Parlaklığı — Krom çıtalardaki mat kireç izlerini çözer.

Neden GYEON Q²M WaterSpot?

• Asidik Güç – Mineral kalıntılarını anında parçalar.
• Kaplama Güvenli – Seramik ve wax’ı bozmaz.
• Zamandan Tasarruf – Polisaj adımını ortadan kaldırır.
• Çok Yönlü & Ekonomik – 25 ml ile tam araç bakımı.

Önerilen Aksesuar & Tamamlayıcı Ürünler

Sıkça Sorulan Sorular

Q: Sıcak panelde kullanabilir miyim?
A: Hayır; yüzey soğuyana kadar bekleyin, aksi hâlde kuruma izi oluşabilir.
Q: Mat boya veya mat PPF’de güvenli mi?
A: Doğru süreyle kullanıldığında iz bırakmaz; kurutmaya izin vermeyin.
Q: Seramik kaplamaya zarar verir mi?
A: Hayır; asidik formül kaplamayı çözmez, yalnızca mineral kalıntıları hedefler.
Q: Ürünü seyreltmem gerekiyor mu?
A: Gerekmiyor; kullanıma hazırdır.

Püskürt, sil, durula – kireç ve su lekeleri tarihe karışsın, parlak yüzeyler anında geri gelsin!

### Nasıl Kullanılır?
1. Aracın temiz ve kuru olduğundan emin olun.
2. 15-20 cm mesafeden lekeye sıkın; panel panel çalışın.
3. Maksimum 30 saniye bekleyin; kurumasına izin vermeyin.
4. Yumuşak mikrofiberle tek yönlü silin.
5. Duru suyla kalıntıları tamamen uzaklaştırın.
6. İnatçı lekede adımları yenileyin.

### Ne Zaman Kullanılır?
Yıkama sonrası su lekesi silme, seramik kaplama bakımı, cam ve ayna kireç çözme, sert su bölgesi bakımı için kullanılır.

### Web Kaynak İçerikleri
> Kaynak 1: https://gyeon.co/product/waterspot/

Q²M WATERSPOT

Exterior / maintenance

Safe solution for removing mineral deposits from any painted exterior surface.

Q²M WaterSpot is a dedicated product designed to remove water spots safely from paintwork. Water spots can appear on fresh coatings due to improper maintenance. Q²M WaterSpot enables the removal of these defects without polishing, and in most cases, without the need to reapply the ceramic coating.

Strong and effective waterspot remover.

Q²M WaterSpot helps correct water spot damage while preserving existing protection layers. It offers a simple solution for restoring surface clarity without aggressive correction methods.

Benefit Icon:
SUITABLE FOR ALL PAINTED SURFACES

Benefit Icon:
EFFECTIVE WATERMARK REMOVER

Benefit Icon:
SLICK AND SMOOTH USAGE

TECHNICAL DETAILS

Technical Image:

CAPACITIES: 500 ML / 1000 ML
BODYWORK SAFE: YES
PH NEUTRAL: NO
COATING SAFE: DEPENDING ON COATING
Consumption: 15ml/panel

HOW TO USE

01 - Wash the vehicle using a pH neutral shampoo and dry the surface.
02 - Spray Q²M WaterSpot onto the paint or a microfibre cloth.
03 - Wipe the affected area gently.
04 - Repeat application for heavier staining if required.
05 - Rinse or wipe the surface with Q²M Prep after use.

FREQUENTLY ASKED QUESTIONS

01 - Is Q²M WaterSpot safe for ceramic coatings?
It is safe in many cases, but coating compatibility depends on the specific coating.

02 - Does it replace polishing?
It does not, but in many cases, it removes water spots without polishing.

03 - Can it be used on fresh coatings?
No, it may permanently reduce the coating performance.

04 - Is it pH neutral?
No, it is an acidic product.

05 - How much product is needed per panel?
One to two sprays are enough.

> Kaynak 2: https://detailarena.com/products/gyeon-q2m-water-spot

GYEON - Q2M Water Spot

Brand: Gyeon Quartz

Price: $13.99

The biggest advantage of Q²M WaterSpot is its safety on paintwork. Due to inappropriate maintenance, water spots may become an issue on fresh coatings. You can remove the most undesirable defects by using Q²M WaterSpot without the need to polish and, in most cases, re-apply the quartz coat.

EASY & EFFECTIVE

Q²M WaterSpot is very easy to use. Before applying, clean the bodywork with a gentle, pH-neutral high-quality shampoo and dry the surface. Then spray directly onto the paint or on a microfiber cloth and wipe the area affected with water spots. If there is strong staining, spray generously directly onto the surface and wipe the surface a few times with a microfiber. Repeat if required.

BEST PRACTICE AND PRO-TIPS

Work panel by panel. Never spray on a large area at once, as the product might dry. Use a soft microfiber and wipe the affected area multiple times. If necessary - repeat the process. TIP: Never leave a towel soaked with the product on the surface, especially glass.

CONSUMPTION: 15ml/panel
COATING SAFE: DEPENDING ON COATING
PH NEUTRAL: NO
BODYWORK SAFE: YES
CAPACITY: 500 ML

Made in South Korea

The biggest advantage of Q²M WaterSpot is its safety on paintwork. Due to inappropriate maintenance, water spots may become an issue on fresh coatings, but there are some quality car washing supplies to help with this. You can remove the most undesirable defects by using Q²M WaterSpot water spot remover spray without the need to polish and, in most cases, re-apply the quartz coat.

EASY AND EFFECTIVE – Q²M WaterSpot is very easy to use. Before applying, clean the bodywork with a gentle, pH neutral high-quality shampoo and dry the surface. Then spray the water spot remover spray directly onto the paint or on a microfiber cloth and wipe the area affected with water spots. If there is strong staining, spray generously directly onto the surface and wipe the surface a few times with a microfiber. Repeat if required.

BREAKS DOWN MINERAL DEPOSITS – Q²M WaterSpot is specifically designed to break down the mineral deposits left behind from rain water. These deposits, once exposed to the sun and heat will etch in to your clear coat causing water spots. Remove them quickly and safely with water spot remover spray.

Gyeon WaterSpot - 500 ml

Price: $14.99

Available Sizes: 500 ml - $14.99

Product Code: GY-1800

Product Information:
- Easily remove water spots and mineral deposits
- Thick formula allows for long work time
- Works great on paint and your glass

Customer Reviews: 67% of customers said that they would buy this item again (Based upon 6 ratings)

Product Description:

Gyeon WaterSpot helps break down and remove mineral deposits left behind by water spots! Unfortunately, water spots can actually etch in to the surface of your paint, glass, etc. and once there, they can be incredibly frustrating and time consuming to remove. The traditional option for removal is to polish the area, starting with a less aggressive polish to a stronger one, however there are now other options you should consider first. If a simple washing doesn't work apply WaterSpot onto the desired surface and wipe away with a clean microfiber towel. If you still have water spots, Gyeon does recommend reapplying a few times for best results and more vigorous wiping. The thick formula allows you to use very little product when applying. It does not diminish or dry quickly, so the area can be wiped multiple times, helping you remove water spots with less product. If you have any coatings already applied, WaterSpot can help you remove water spots in the paint without having to polish or reapply your coating. Gyeon does share a warning: "WaterSpot might affect the hydrophobic layer of a coating. It's dangerous to leave the product on the paint and especially on glass for a long time". With that advice, we always recommend applying this product in the shade and once finished washing the area with a car wash shampoo like the Gyeon Bathe or Bathe+. Don't let ugly water spots take away from the overall luster of your vehicle, use Gyeon WaterSpot to take care of them!

Important: This item cannot be shipped, sold, or used in the state of California. CARB in California claims this item breaks their VOC regulations.

> Kaynak 6: https://www.cleanyourcar.co.uk/gyeon-water-spot-remover

GYEON - Q²M WaterSpot Remover

9 Reviews

GYEON Q2M Water Spot Remover is an effective solution for removing unsightly water spotting deposits from paintwork. GYEON Q2M Water spot is a mild acid cleaner that gently dissolves these deposits from the paintwork.

Brand: GYEON

Pricing:
- 500ml: £11.50 inc. vat (Stock: 17)
- 1000ml: £17.00 inc. vat (Stock: 13)

Product Images:
-
-

GYEON Q2M Water Spot Remover is an effective solution for removing unsightly water spotting deposits from paintwork.

Water spotting occurs in hard water areas and from regular rainfall as the water evaporates from the surface leaving behind calcium and mineral deposits, a problem that is most obvious in summer. GYEON Q2M Water spot is a mild acid cleaner that gently dissolves these deposits from the paintwork.

GYEON Q2M Water Spot remover is very easy to use. Before applying, clean the bodywork with a gentle, pH-neutral shampoo such as Gyeon Bathe and dry the surface. Then spray directly onto the paint or on a microfiber cloth and wipe the area affected with water spots. If there is strong staining, spray generously directly onto the surface and wipe the surface a few times with a microfibre. If required - repeat.

GYEON Q2M WaterSpot is thick and oily, so very little product is required to cover a large area. It does not diminish or dry fast, so the cleaned area can be wiped multiple times.

Features & Benefits:
- Dissolves water spot marks quickly
- Ideal for use on vehicles protected with nanotechnology-based quartz coatings
- Particularly useful for freshly applied nanotechnology-based quartz coatings
- Lubricating oils reduce chances of marring paintwork
- Pre-diluted - ready to use

Technical Specification:
- Bodywork safe
- Quartz coating safe
- Mildly acidic (pH 4-5)
- Coverage: 15ml / panel

Using Gyeon Q2M WaterSpot:

Ensure vehicle is clean and dry before use. For a deep clean Gyeon Q2M Restart Wash is a good starting point. Mist Q2M WaterSpot on to the panel, allow it to dwell for a few seconds and wipe with a soft microfibre towel. On fresh spots, mist Q2M WaterSpot on to a towel and wipe. Once complete, wash the vehicle down with shampoo.

Use on all exterior surfaces except for glass. Q2M WaterSpot can cause damage on glass and exterior surfaces if allowed to dry. Keep out of reach of children and use in a well ventilated area.

Available in 1 Litre & 500ml Bottle with sprayer

### Detaylı Açıklama
100% SCALE; SU İZİ TEMİZLEYİCİ KIREÇ SÖKÜCÜ ve ÖNLEYİCİ

100% SCALE; Kaporta, jantlar, motor bölmesi, cam (panoramik sunroof), plastik ve polikarbonat gibi tüm dış araç yüzeylerinde mevcut kireç, tuz lekeleri, asit yağmuru ve hafif yüzey oksidasyonu üzerinde yoğun ve enerjik bir dekontaminasyon eyleminin/temizliğinin gerekli olduğu durumlarda kullanım için geliştirilmiş yeni nesil asit pH ürünüdür.

100% SCALE; Dekontamine edici kimyasal etkisine ek olarak, eski seramik kaplama ve koruyucu tabaka işlemlerini kaldırmak için kullanılabilir, böylece yeni veya kullanılmış araçlarda yüzeyi yeni bir koruyucu döngünün/tabakanın uygulanması için hazırlar.

100% SCALE; Su bazlı formülasyonu hem kuru hem de ıslak yüzeylerde kolay uygulama sağlar. İçeriğindeki özel maddeler sayesinde buharlaşma azalır, uzun bir işlenebilirlik ve sonuç olarak derinlemesine bir etki sağlar.

100% SCALE; EDTA/NTA ve ilave fosfor* içermez.

KULLANIM TALIMATI
• 100% SCALE ile Her seferinde bir panel üzerinde çalışmanızı öneririz.
• 100% SCALE soğuk yüzeylere ve doğrudan güneş almayan ortamlarda kullanılmalıdır. Ürünü yüzeye püskürtün ve birkaç dakika bekletin, dikey ve yatay hareketlerle yaymak için bir mikrofiber aplikatör veya yumuşak kıllı bir fırça kullanın. Ardından yüksek basınçlı su/bol su ile durulayın.
• Taze Kireç, mineral kalıntıları ve yeni asit yağmurlarından olağan temizlik için: 100% SCALE 1:5 oranında sulandırarak kullanın.
• Eski ve yerleşmiş Kireç, mineral kalıntıları ve eski asit yağmurlarından olağanüstü temizlik veya eski koruyucu kaplamaların çıkarılması için: 100% SCALE saf olarak kullanın.
• Cam ve farların olağanüstü temizliği: 100% SCALE saf olarak kullanın.

UYARILAR
• Sıcak yüzeylere veya güneş altında uygulanmasını tavsiye etmiyoruz.
• Uygulama sonrası ürünün yüzeyde kurumasına izin vermeyiniz.
• Cam veya diğer yüzeylerde uzun süre kalmasına izin verilmemesini tavsiye ederiz.
• Güçlü bir dekontaminasyon özelliği nedeniyle, 100% SCALE direnci bilinmeyen önceden uygulanmış koruyucu tabakalar/işlemler üzerinde saf olarak kullanılmasını önermiyoruz. Bu gibi durumlarda 1: 5 veya daha fazla bir seyreltme öneririz
• 100% SCALE anti-korozifler içerse bile boyasız veya aside duyarlı yüzeylerde (örn. doğrudan parlak vernikler) saf olarak kullanmayın.
• Şüphe durumunda veya özellikle hassas yüzeylerde, kullanmadan önce uygulamanın küçük bir gizli parça üzerinde test edilmesi her zaman tavsiye edilir.
• Her zaman MSDS'ye ve etiket üzerindeki önlemlere ve talimatlara bakın.
• Ürünü daha önce SP1 Prewash ve DS Scale ile temizlenmiş yüzeylerde kullanmanızı öneririz.

\n\n\n\n# InnovaCar DS Scale 1L\n\nSKU: 79290\n\nRegular price: \u20ac17,07 EUR\n\nStatus: Sold out / Out of stock\n\n## THE BENEFITS OF DS SCALE\n\nDS Scale by Innovacar is the specific car and decontaminating shampoo to treat and combat water spots and limescale stains on the body: \"the classic annoying white spots\".\n\nLimescale, is deposited on the bodywork in the form of microparticles that are not always visible to the naked eye, causing a microlayer over the nanotechnology and protective films. Over time, this reduces the effectiveness of the protections and water repellency of the sealant and ceramic products and thus leads the operator to believe that such treatments must be performed from scratch.\n\nThis is where DS Scale comes into play, the purifying and descaling shampoo perfect to fight the accumulated limescale layer and contaminations, allowing the nanotechnological protections to reactivate themselves.\n\nDs Scale has the following features:\n\n- 2-in-1 car shampoo: it is the perfect solution for the washing phase, that is, as a purifying shampoo to be used about every 4 cleaning cycles. Otherwise, when used pure or more concentrated, DS Scale is a decontaminant for limestone and minerals that can be applied to stubborn water or acid rain stains or for extraordinary intervention.\n\n- Frees the coating and protections: by removing the limescale surface layer and the contamination, it prolongs the lifespan of the protective layers previously applied.\n\n- Does not affect protective films: even when used pure or more concentrated for decontamination of limestone or other contamination, DS Scale does not affect the protective layers on the bodywork.\n\n- Suitable for windows, headlights and emblems: it can also be used to remove limescale residues from glass, headlights, hard external plastics or car decorative elements such as emblems, lettering and aluminium or metal details.\n\nAverage consumption:\n\n- For extraordinary decontamination: 15 ml per brush.\n\n- For maintenance: 20 ml per vehicle.\n\nSummarised technical data:\n\n- Limescale cleaning: 5/5\n\n- Mineral cleaning: 5/5\n\n- Cleaning action: 5/5\n\n- Coating safety: YES\n\n- Surface safety: YES\n\n- pH: 3.00\n\n## DS SCALE IS IDEAL FOR\n\n- Cleaning the car, prolonging polishing and coating effects.\n\n- Purifying surfaces by removing limescale, water and contamination stains.\n\n- Dealing with extraordinary decontamination following acid rain.\n\n- Having a solution that can be used on multiple parts of the car such as windows, hard plastics and body.\n\n- Having a product that can be used for multiple purposes, according to different needs.\n\n- Excellent for decontaminating and purifying car windows, preparing them in the best possible way for the application of the coating and for the water-repellent treatment with SC3 Glass Sealant.\n\nSKU: 102563

In addition, these characteristics facilitate direct application only in small areas where there is contamination to be treated;\n\n- Easy application: thanks to its water-based formulation, the product can be used on both wet and dry surfaces;\n\n- Eliminates old protective coatings: it can be used to eliminate old protective and ceramic treatments previously applied and almost at the end of their life. This can prepare the surface, of new or used cars, for the application of a new protective cycle;\n\n- Preparation of glass for protective treatments: if applied to windows and glass prior to the application of SC3 Glass Sealant, it allows the surface to be cleaned and prepared for protection;\n\n- Safety: it contains no EDTA/NTA and no added phosphorous*.\n\nAverage consumption: 150 ml per car or 15-20 ml per panel.\n\nSummary technical data:\n\n- Limescale cleaning: 5/5\n\n- Mineral cleaning: 5/5\n\n- Decontaminant: 5/5\n\n- Cleaning action: 5/5\n\n- Surface safety: YES\n\n- pH: 1.5\n\n* May contain traces.\n\n## 100% SCALES IS IDEAL FOR\n\n- Remove annoying limescale, salt and acid rain stains from glass, bodywork and exterior car surfaces;\n\n- Chemically dissolve contamination to simplify the polishing process and thus shorten its time;\n\n- Remove protectives already present on a car, to avoid interference with a new nanotechnological treatment, different from the previous one;\n\n- Prepare the glass and crystal surface as well as possible before applying a specific protective agent such as SC3 Glass Sealant.\n\n## HOW TO USE 100% SCALE\n\nFor extraordinary cleaning against limescale, mineral residues and old acid rain stains or for removing old protective coatings:\n\n- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.\n\n- It is recommended to prepare the surface to be treated with 100% Scale through a prewash phase with SP1 Prewash and a wash phase with DS Scale.\n\n- Use a microfiber applicator and spread the product with light pressure and vertical and horizontal movements, leaving it to act for a couple of minutes.\n\n- Proceed to rinse with water, even at high pressure.\n\nFor ordinary cleaning of limescale and mineral residues and recent acid rain:\n\n- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.\n\n- Spray the product diluted 1:5, treating one panel at a time, leaving it to act for a couple of minutes.\n\n- For a more intense action: use a soft bristle brush and spread the product with vertical and horizontal movements.\n\n- Proceed to rinse with water, even at high pressure.\n\nFor extraordinary cleaning of windows and headlights:\n\n- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.\n\n- It is recommended to prepare the surface to be treated with 100% Scale through a prewash phase with SP1 Prewash and a wash phase with DS Scale.\n\n- Spread the product onto the glass with a microfiber applicator evenly and allow it to work for a couple of minutes.\n\n- For more intense action: use a medium bristle brush or the white side of Micron Scrub and spread the product with vertical and horizontal movements.\n\n- Wait a couple of minutes and rinse.\n\nExtraordinary cleaning: use the product pure.\n\nFor ordinary cleaning of limescale, mineral residues and recent acid rain: dilution can be up to 1:5, i.e. use 160 ml of product and fill the remaining part with water (840 ml) to obtain 1 L of ready-to-use solution.\n\nWarnings:\n\nWe advise not to apply on hot surfaces or in the sun and not to allow the product to dry out or remain on glass or other surfaces for a long time.\n\nWe do not recommend using the product pure on previously applied protective treatments whose resistance is unknown, as it is a strong decontaminating treatment. In such cases we recommend a dilution of 1:5 or more.\n\nDo not use pure on unpainted or acid-sensitive surfaces (i.e. direct gloss varnishes), even if the product contains anti-corrosives.\n\nIf in doubt or on particularly sensitive surfaces, it is always recommended to test the application on a small hidden part before use.\n\nAlways refer to the MSDS and the precautions and instructions on the label.\n\nWe recommend using the product on surfaces previously cleaned with SP1 Prewash and DS Scale.

INNOVACAR 0 SCALE Su İzi Temizleyici Kireç Çözücü ve Önleyici Konsantre – (4,54 Lt)

INNOVACAR 0 SCALE’İN FAYDALARI | Asidik Güç, Derin Dekontaminasyon

Innovacar 0 SCALE, araç yüzeylerindeki kireç izleri, su lekeleri, tuz kalıntıları, asit yağmuru ve hafif oksidasyon gibi inatçı kirleri çözmek üzere formüle edilmiş konsantre bir asidik dekontaminanttır. Hem klasik temizlik hem de seramik kaplama öncesi hazırlık işlemleri için uygundur.
• Derinlemesine Kireç Temizliği: Cam, kaporta, jant, motor bölmesi, plastik ve polikarbonat yüzeylerde yoğun bir dekontaminasyon sağlar.
• Koruyucu Katman Sökücüsü: Yüzeydeki yaşlı seramik veya koruyucu tabakaları çıkartarak yeni uygulamalar için zemini hazırlar.
• Jel Formül & Yavaş Buharlaşma: Yüzeyde daha uzun süre çalışır, dikey alanlarda akma yapmadan etki eder.
• EDTA / NTA / Fosfor İçermez: Çevreye ve kullanıcıya karşı daha güvenlidir.
• Islak veya Kuru Uygulama: Su bazlı yapısıyla her iki durumda da kolay kullanım sunar.
Ortalama Tüketim:
• Tüm araç için: 150 ml
• Panel başına: 15–20 ml
pH: 1.5 (güçlü asidik)

0 SCALE NASIL KULLANILIR? | Uygulama Talimatları
1. Uygulama yapılacak yüzeyin soğuk ve gölgede olduğundan emin olun.
2. Her seferinde tek bir panel üzerinde çalışın.
3. Ürünü yüzeye püskürtün, birkaç dakika bekletin.
4. Mikrofiber aplikatör veya yumuşak fırça ile dikey-yatay hareketlerle yaydırın.
5. Bol su ile (tercihen basınçlı) durulayın.

Kullanım Senaryoları:
• Yeni kireç lekeleri ve hafif kalıntılar: 1:5 oranında seyreltin.
• Eski, inatçı lekeler veya koruyucu tabaka sökümü: Saf kullanın.
• Cam ve far temizliği: Saf olarak kullanılır.

Uyarılar:
• Sıcak yüzeylerde ve güneş altında uygulamayın.
• Ürünü yüzeyde kurutmayın.
• Aşırı hassas, boyasız veya aside duyarlı alanlarda saf kullanım önerilmez.
• Belirsiz yüzeylerde önce küçük bir alanda test edin.
• MSDS ve ürün etiketinde yer alan güvenlik önlemlerine uyun.

## THE BENEFITS OF 100% SCALE

100% Scale by Innovacar is a new generation acid pH product that can be used as a car limescale remover for an intense and energetic decontaminating action on limescale, salt stains, acid rain and slight surface oxidation on all external vehicle surfaces.

It is a decontaminant developed with a sophisticated medium viscosity formula designed to make application easy even on vertical surfaces and to become an essential support in the difficult task of limescale or water spot mineral stains removal, from vehicle surfaces.

Main features:

- Intense decontamination: thanks to its special substances, it can treat the most serious limescale and salt contamination and has a slower evaporation rate, allowing it to be worked with brushes, cloths and applicators for a long time;
- Can be used on the exterior surfaces of the car: it can be used on body parts, wheels, the engine compartment, plastics and also on glass, the panoramic sunroof, headlights and polycarbonate;
- Gel formula and reduction of drippings: thanks to its viscosity, it is made to cling more tightly to the sides and vertical surfaces, facilitating workability and thus reducing drippings. In addition, these characteristics facilitate direct application only in small areas where there is contamination to be treated;
- Easy application: thanks to its water-based formulation, the product can be used on both wet and dry surfaces;
- Eliminates old protective coatings: it can be used to eliminate old protective and ceramic treatments previously applied and almost at the end of their life. This can prepare the surface, of new or used cars, for the application of a new protective cycle;
- Preparation of glass for protective treatments: if applied to windows and glass prior to the application of SC3 Glass Sealant, it allows the surface to be cleaned and prepared for protection;
- Safety: it contains no EDTA/NTA and no added phosphorous*.

Average consumption: 150 ml per car or 15-20 ml per panel.

Summary technical data:
- Limescale cleaning: 5/5
- Mineral cleaning: 5/5
- Decontaminant: 5/5
- Cleaning action: 5/5
- Surface safety: YES
- pH: 1.5

* May contain traces.

## 100% SCALES IS IDEAL FOR

- Remove annoying limescale, salt and acid rain stains from glass, bodywork and exterior car surfaces;
- Chemically dissolve contamination to simplify the polishing process and thus shorten its time;
- Remove protectives already present on a car, to avoid interference with a new nanotechnological treatment, different from the previous one;
- Prepare the glass and crystal surface as well as possible before applying a specific protective agent such as SC3 Glass Sealant.

## HOW TO USE 100% SCALE

For extraordinary cleaning against limescale, mineral residues and old acid rain stains or for removing old protective coatings:
- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.
- It is recommended to prepare the surface to be treated with 100% Scale through a prewash phase with SP1 Prewash and a wash phase with DS Scale.
- Use a microfiber applicator and spread the product with light pressure and vertical and horizontal movements, leaving it to act for a couple of minutes.
- Proceed to rinse with water, even at high pressure.

For ordinary cleaning of limescale and mineral residues and recent acid rain:
- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.
- Spray the product diluted 1:5, treating one panel at a time, leaving it to act for a couple of minutes.
- For a more intense action: use a soft bristle brush and spread the product with vertical and horizontal movements.
- Proceed to rinse with water, even at high pressure.

For extraordinary cleaning of windows and headlights:
- Wait until surfaces are cool and apply away from the sun.
- It is recommended to prepare the surface to be treated with 100% Scale through a prewash phase with SP1 Prewash and a wash phase with DS Scale.
- Spread the product onto the glass with a microfiber applicator evenly and allow it to work for a couple of minutes.
- For more intense action: use a medium bristle brush or the white side of Micron Scrub and spread the product with vertical and horizontal movements.
- Wait a couple of minutes and rinse.

Extraordinary cleaning: use the product pure.

For ordinary cleaning of limescale, mineral residues and recent acid rain: dilution can be up to 1:5, i.e. use 160 ml of product and fill the remaining part with water (840 ml) to obtain 1 L of ready-to-use solution.

Warnings:
We advise not to apply on hot surfaces or in the sun and not to allow the product to dry out or remain on glass or other surfaces for a long time.
We do not recommend using the product pure on previously applied protective treatments whose resistance is unknown, as it is a strong decontaminating treatment. In such cases we recommend a dilution of 1:5 or more.
Do not use pure on unpainted or acid-sensitive surfaces (i.e. direct gloss varnishes), even if the product contains anti-corrosives.
If in doubt or on particularly sensitive surfaces, it is always recommended to test the application on a small hidden part before use.
Always refer to the MSDS and the precautions and instructions on the label.
We recommend using the product on surfaces previously cleaned with SP1 Prewash and DS Scale.
